# OSLSR Public Website - Information Architecture

**Version:** 1.0
**Date:** 2026-01-18
**Status:** COMPLETE - All Sections Documented
**Source Documents:** PRD v7.5, Architecture v7.4, UX Spec v2.0, homepage_structure.md, salvaged session documents

---

## Document Purpose

This document is the **single source of truth** for the OSLSR public website. It contains:
- Full page wireframes with actual content copy
- Navigation structure (header, footer, mobile)
- Visual step flows and user journeys
- Phase 1 (static) vs Phase 2 (API-dependent) breakdown
- Component requirements

All implementation must reference this document.

---

## Key Decisions Log

Decisions made during planning sessions, preserved here for reference:

| Decision | Choice | Rationale |
|----------|--------|-----------|
| ID Cards | Staff-only (Supervisors, Enumerators) | Prevents abuse/duplication; NIN is the government-approved ID |
| Public Recognition | Verified Badge on profile | Digital recognition without physical card risks |
| Photo Required | No (for public registration) | Reduces friction; not needed without ID card |
| CTA Strategy | Option D: Smart button + Staff Portal in footer | Clean header, security through obscurity for staff |
| Help Center | Merged into Support section | Reduces navigation complexity |
| Privacy Page | Under About section | Trust-building content belongs with institutional info |

---

## 1. Navigation Hierarchy

### 1.1 Header Navigation (Primary)

```

â”‚                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  [Oyo State Crest]  OSLSR    About   Participate   Marketplace   Insights   Support    [Register Now]
â”‚                                                                                     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Logo Area (Left)**
- Oyo State Government Crest
- "OSLSR" text (expands to "Oyo State Labour & Skills Registry" on hover/focus)
- Links to homepage (/)

**Primary Navigation (Center)**

| Nav Item | URL | Dropdown Items |
|----------|-----|----------------|
| About | /about | The Initiative, How It Works, Leadership, Partners, Privacy & Data Protection |
| Participate | /participate | For Workers, For Employers |
| Marketplace | /marketplace | _(No dropdown - direct link)_ |
| Insights | /insights | Skills Map, Trends, Reports |
| Support | /support | FAQ, Guides, Contact, Verify a Worker |

**CTA Area (Right) - Option D: Smart Context-Aware Button**

| User State | Button Display | Action |
|------------|----------------|--------|
| Not logged in, no cookie | `[Register Now]` | â†’ /register |
| Has incomplete survey (cookie/localStorage) | `[Continue Survey]` | â†’ /login (then redirect to survey) |
| Logged in | `[Dashboard]` or `[My Profile]` | â†’ /dashboard or /profile |

### 1.4 Complete Route Map

**Public Content Pages:**

| Route | Page | Phase |
|-------|------|-------|
| `/` | Homepage | 1 |
| `/about` | About Landing | 1 |
| `/about/initiative` | The Initiative | 1 |
| `/about/how-it-works` | How It Works | 1 |
| `/about/leadership` | Leadership | 1 |
| `/about/partners` | Partners | 1 |
| `/about/privacy` | Privacy & Data Protection | 1 |
| `/participate` | Participate Landing | 1 |
| `/participate/workers` | For Workers | 1 |
| `/participate/employers` | For Employers | 1 |
| `/marketplace` | Marketplace | 2 |
| `/marketplace/profile/:id` | Worker Profile | 2 |
| `/insights` | Insights Dashboard | 2 |
| `/insights/skills-map` | Skills Map | 2 |
| `/insights/trends` | Trends | 2 |
| `/insights/reports` | Reports | 2 |
| `/support` | Support Landing | 1 |
| `/support/faq` | FAQ | 1 |
| `/support/guides` | Guides | 1 |
| `/support/contact` | Contact | 1 |
| `/support/verify-worker` | Verify a Worker | 1 |

**Functional Pages:**

| Route | Page | Phase |
|-------|------|-------|
| `/register` | Public Registration | 1 |
| `/login` | Public Login | 1 |
| `/verify-email` | Email Verification | 1 |
| `/forgot-password` | Password Reset Request | 1 |
| `/reset-password` | Password Reset | 1 |
| `/survey` | Survey (Enketo) | 1 |
| `/survey/complete` | Survey Complete | 1 |
| `/staff/login` | Staff Login | 1 |
| `/terms` | Terms of Service | 1 |

---

### 4.2 /participate/workers - For Workers

**Key Content Decisions:**
- No mention of ID cards (staff-only decision)
- Verified badge explained as profile indicator
- No photo required explicitly stated
- Two-stage consent explained (marketplace + contact visibility)
- Clear FAQ section addressing common concerns

**Key Content Decisions:**
- Clear explanation of what verification means (and doesn't mean)
- Data visibility table shows what's public vs requires registration
- Emphasis on free service
- Honest disclaimer about skills vs identity verification
- Embedded search at bottom (mirrors homepage marketplace preview)

---

### Participate Section Summary

| Page | URL | Purpose | Content Type | Phase |
|------|-----|---------|--------------|-------|
| Landing | /participate | Route to worker/employer path | Static | 1 |
| For Workers | /participate/workers | Benefits, requirements, registration CTA | Static | 1 |
| For Employers | /participate/employers | How to find talent, verification explained | Static + Search placeholder | 1 (search Phase 2) |

**All Phase 1 â€” marketplace search on employer page follows same feature flag pattern as homepage.**

### 5.5 /support/verify-worker - Verify a Worker

**Purpose:** Public verification tool to confirm a worker's OSLSR registration status.

**Note:** This feature is implemented in Story 1-6.


- Public (all visitors): Skill, LGA, Experience Level, Verified Badge

- Never public: NIN, Email, Full Address

- Marketplace consent data
- Read-only replica for performance (per architecture)

- Aggregation pipeline for anonymized metrics

- Rate limiting (3 attempts, then lockout)
- No self-service password reset (contact supervisor)
- Session timeout: 30 minutes
- IP logging for audit

### Functional Pages Summary

| Page | URL | Purpose | Phase |
|------|-----|---------|-------|
| Register | /register | Create worker account | 1 |
| Verify Email | /verify-email | Email confirmation | 1 |
| Login | /login | Public user login | 1 |
| Forgot Password | /forgot-password | Password reset request | 1 |
| Reset Password | /reset-password | Set new password | 1 |
| Survey | /survey | Enketo skills survey | 1 |
| Survey Complete | /survey/complete | Post-survey confirmation | 1 |
| Staff Login | /staff/login | Staff authentication | 1 |
| Terms | /terms | Terms of service | 1 |

**All Phase 1 content.**

---

## 9. Phase Breakdown

### Phase 1: Static Content (Buildable Now)

- Homepage shell (hero, sections, CTAs)
- All About sub-pages
- All Participate sub-pages
- Support section (FAQ, Guides, Contact)
- Verify Worker tool (Story 1-6 completed)
- Registration flow
- Login flow
- Legal pages

### Phase 2: API-Dependent (Epic 7+)

- Marketplace search
- Worker profiles
- Insights dashboard
- Skills map
- Trends/Reports
- Profile management
- Live metrics on homepage

---

## 10. Component Inventory

Based on the page wireframes above, these are the reusable UI components needed.

### 10.1 Navigation Components

| Component | Description | Used On |
|-----------|-------------|---------|
| `Header` | Primary navigation with logo, nav items, CTA button | All pages |
| `HeaderNavItem` | Nav item with optional dropdown | Header |
| `HeaderDropdown` | Dropdown menu for nav sections | About, Participate, Insights, Support |
| `MobileNav` | Slide-out mobile navigation drawer | All pages (mobile) |
| `Footer` | Site footer with links, legal, staff portal | All pages |
| `Breadcrumb` | Path navigation for sub-pages | Sub-pages |

### 10.2 Hero & Section Components

| Component | Description | Used On |
|-----------|-------------|---------|
| `HeroSection` | Full-width hero with heading, subheading, CTAs | Homepage, landing pages |
| `SectionHeader` | Section title with optional description | All content sections |
| `SectionDivider` | Visual separator between sections | All pages |

| `GuideCard` | Card for step-by-step guides | Support/Guides |
| `WorkerCard` | Marketplace worker preview card | Marketplace search |
| `StatCard` | Single metric display (number + label) | Homepage, Insights |

---

### Component Design Tokens

For consistency, all components should use these design tokens:

**Colors:**
- Primary: Oyo State green (from government branding)
- Secondary: Complementary blue
- Success: Green
- Warning: Amber
- Error: Red
- Neutral: Gray scale

**Typography:**
- Headings: Sans-serif (e.g., Inter, Poppins)
- Body: Same sans-serif at smaller weights
- Sizes: Responsive scale

**Spacing:**
- Base unit: 4px
- Section padding: 64px vertical (desktop), 32px (mobile)
- Content max-width: 1200px

**Breakpoints:**
- Mobile: < 640px
- Tablet: 640px - 1024px
- Desktop: > 1024px

---

### Implementation Priority

**Phase 1 (Must Have):**
1. Navigation components (Header, Footer, MobileNav)
2. Form components (all)
3. Content components (StepFlow, FAQAccordion, InfoBox)
4. Card components (FeatureCard, AudienceCard)
5. Action components (all buttons)
6. Verification components

**Phase 2 (After Launch):**
1. Marketplace components
2. Insights components
3. Advanced filtering

### B.2 Logo & Favicon Implementation

**Logo Source:**
- Downloaded from official Oyo State Government website: `https://oyostate.gov.ng`
- Logo includes the official coat of arms with "OYO STATE - THE PACESETTER STATE" text

**Files Created:**

| File Path | Description | Size |
|-----------|-------------|------|
| `apps/web/public/images/oyo-state-logo.png` | Full color logo | 19.6 KB |
| `apps/web/public/images/oyo-state-logo-white.png` | White variant for dark backgrounds | 17.4 KB |
| `apps/web/public/images/oyo-state-logo.svg` | Auto-traced SVG of full logo | 45.8 KB |
| `apps/web/public/images/oyo-coat-of-arms.png` | Extracted coat of arms only | 354 KB |
| `apps/web/public/images/oyo-coat-of-arms.svg` | Auto-traced SVG of coat of arms | 154 KB |
| `apps/web/public/favicon-16x16.png` | Browser tab icon | 811 B |
| `apps/web/public/favicon-32x32.png` | Browser tab icon (retina) | 2.5 KB |
| `apps/web/public/favicon-48x48.png` | Windows taskbar | 4.8 KB |
| `apps/web/public/apple-touch-icon.png` | iOS home screen icon | 50 KB |
| `apps/web/public/android-chrome-192x192.png` | Android home screen | 57 KB |
| `apps/web/public/android-chrome-512x512.png` | Android splash screen | 354 KB |
| `apps/web/public/site.webmanifest` | PWA manifest file | - |

**Utility Scripts Created:**

| Script | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `apps/web/scripts/generate-favicons.mjs` | Generates all favicon sizes from source logo using sharp |
| `apps/web/scripts/convert-to-svg.mjs` | Converts PNG logos to SVG using potrace |

**Usage:**
```bash
# Regenerate favicons if logo changes
cd apps/web && node scripts/generate-favicons.mjs

# Regenerate SVGs
cd apps/web && node scripts/convert-to-svg.mjs
```

---

### B.3 Package Dependencies Added

**Web App (`apps/web/package.json`):**

```json
{
  "devDependencies": {
    "sharp": "^0.33.5",    // Image processing for favicon generation
    "potrace": "^2.1.8"    // PNG to SVG conversion (bitmap tracing)
  }
}
```

**Installation:**
```bash
cd apps/web
pnpm add -D sharp potrace
```

---

### B.4 Files Modified

**`apps/web/index.html`**

Added favicon links and meta tags:

```html
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
  <title>OSLSR - Oyo State Labour & Skills Registry</title>

  <!-- Favicons -->
  <link rel="icon" type="image/png" sizes="32x32" href="/favicon-32x32.png" />
  <link rel="icon" type="image/png" sizes="16x16" href="/favicon-16x16.png" />
  <link rel="apple-touch-icon" sizes="180x180" href="/apple-touch-icon.png" />

  <!-- PWA / Android -->
  <link rel="manifest" href="/site.webmanifest" />
  <meta name="theme-color" content="#8B0000" />

  <!-- Meta -->
  <meta name="description" content="Oyo State Labour & Skills Registry - Register your skills and connect with employers across Oyo State" />
</head>
```

### B.5 Logo Usage in Components

**In React/TSX:**
```tsx
// Full logo (header)

// White logo (footer on dark background)
<img src="/images/oyo-state-logo-white.png" alt="Oyo State Logo" />

// SVG logo (scalable)
<img src="/images/oyo-state-logo.svg" alt="Oyo State Logo" />

// Coat of arms only
<img src="/images/oyo-coat-of-arms.png" alt="Oyo State Coat of Arms" />
```

---

### B.6 Notes & Recommendations

**SVG Quality:**
- The auto-traced SVGs are functional but not perfect vector reproductions
- For production quality, recommend:
  1. Requesting official SVG files from Ministry of Labour
  2. Having a designer manually recreate in Figma/Illustrator
  3. Using the PNG versions which are from the official source

**Favicon Sizes:**
- All standard sizes covered for modern browsers
- PWA manifest included for installable web app support
- Theme color set to dark red (#8B0000) matching Oyo State branding

**Public Folder Structure:**
